id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_body" class="ajax__tab_body ajax__scroll_vert"> <div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlFeatures" class="ajax__tab_panel" style="visibility: visible;"> <div class="Features"> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlFeatures_ProductFeatureDesc"><h2><font style="color: #000000;" size="3"><strong><span>BUSHMASTER</span></strong></font></h2> <h2><font style="color: #000000;" size="3"><strong><span>Patrolman AR15 M4 Carbine, .223/5.56 16" W/Detachable Carry Handle, Telescoping Stock, Black Finish 30 Round Mag</span></strong></font></h2> <p><font face="book antiqua,palatino" size="3"><span>Chrome lined barrel and chamber. Features A2 bird cage style suppressor. A3 type removable carry handle features 1 MOA elevation and 1/2 MOA windage adjustments. Picatinny type rail base. Flat-top upper receiver. Non-reflective mil spec hard anodized aluminum receiver. Six-position telestock. Shipped with 30 round magazine, chamber flag and operator's manual.</span></font></p> <p><span>One of our ALL TIME BEST Carbine models, the M4 Type features a distinctive Military Barrel Profile and Six Position Telestock great for 3 Gun Match Shooting, Home Defense and Law Enforcement use.</span></p> <p><span>The Bushmaster A2 &amp; A3 Type Patrolmans Carbines are modeled after our M4 Type Carbines, but with additional barrel length to make them legal for sale to individual officers (semi-automatic configuration with 16" barrel).</span></p> <p><span>The 5.56mm/.223 Rem. caliber 16" barrel is chrome lined in both bore and chamber for long wear life and ease of maintenance. For control of muzzle flash and muzzle rise in rapid fire, a birdcage type suppressor is factory installed. A mil. spec. manganese phosphate outer coating insures protection against corrosion or rust on the barrel and all critical steel parts of the weapon.&nbsp;</span><br> <br><font size="2"> Forged, lightweight 7075T6 aircraft quality aluminum receivers are designed for simplicity of maintenance and reliability of operation and they incorporate all M16A2 design improvements including cartridge case deflector, bolt catch assembly and raised ribs for protection against accidental magazine release. A six position telescoping buttstock offers light weight, carrying ease and quick handling. </font><br> <br><font size="2"> The telestock, pistol grip and two piece handguards are all molded of strong black thermoset composite material. The handguards are internally shielded against barrel heat build-up. The dual aperture M16A2 rear sight system on these carbines offer both windage and elevation adjustment calibrated in meters. </font><br> <br><font style="color: #ff0000;" size="2"> The A3 Type Patrolmans Carbine includes a Removable Carry Handle - adjustment range is from from 300 to 600 meters (1/2 M.o.A. elevation and 1/2 M.o.A. windage).</font><br> <br><font size="2"> Once the Carry Handle is removed, a wide variety of scopes, red dot or holographic sights, or night vision equipment may be mounted on the Upper Receivers integral Picatinny rail. Iron sight zero is completely repeatable when the handle is reattached by means of its knurled knobs. </font><br> <br><font size="2"> The Bushmaster A2/A3 Type Patrolmans Carbines are shipped complete with 30 round magazine, safety and operational manual.</font></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><font size="2">Roll mouse over image to see the full rifle:</font></p> <p><font size="2"><img src="../../../../Data/Default/Images/uploads/bushmaster/bm_90289.jpg" alt="" width="1649" height="530"><br></font></p></span></div> </div><div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_TabSpecifications" class="ajax__tab_panel" style="display:none;visibility:hidden;"> <div class="Features"> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_TabSpecifications_ProductsSpecifications"><ul> <li>Category : Tactical Rifles</li> <li>Action : Semi-Automatic</li> <li>Caliber : 223 Remington/5.56 NATO</li> <li>Barrel Length : 16.0"</li> <li>Capacity : 30+1</li> <li>Trigger : Single Stage</li> <li>Safety : Lever</li> <li>OAL : 32.5"-34.75"</li> <li>Weight : 6.7 lbs</li> <li>Stock Description : 6-Position Black</li> <li>Metal Finish : Black</li> </ul></span></div> </div><div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews" class="ajax__tab_panel" style="display:none;visibility:hidden;"> <div class="Reviews"> <div id="Review"> <div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_UpdatePnlProductReviewDetails"> <div class="Sorting"> <span class="TitleStyle"> Reviewed by <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_CustomersCnt">13</span> customer </span>&nbsp; Let's see I bought it back in 2007 and it has never failed, once, ever. I've feed it FMJ's, softpoints, hollow points, nearly every brand you can imagine, PMC, Federal, Remington, Winchester, Hornady.... not one hiccup. Granted these are all quality ammo manufacturers, will it feed Wolf, Silver Bear? I'm not sure and I don't intend to find out. This rifle is everything an AR-15 should be. It's well built, fit on the upper and lower is very tight. Barrel is chrome lined, Trigger is good enough for all practical shooting applications. If you want to use this rifle to snipe joe badguy from 400 yards away then by all means get a better trigger, but for the type of shooting most people do or might be forced to do, this weapon out of the box is more than you will ever need. Last but not least value. You can easily buy two of these rifles for what some manufacturers are asking for one. I've stood side by side with guys that have LMT's, POF's, Wilson Combat's, I've never felt out gunned. 1000's of rounds fired not one failure... I might be the luckiest son of a gun in town but this rifle is still king.</div> <div class="Row"> By <span class="Text"> kyle</span> from <span class="Text"> Gillette, WY</span></div> </div> </div> </td> </tr> </tbody></table> </div> <div class="Paging"> <div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_topNavigation"> <a id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_TopPrevLink" disabled="disabled"> Previous</a> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_lblPagingInfo"> | PAGE1 of 2 | </span> <a id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_TopNextLink" href="javascript:__doPostBack('ctl00$ctl00$MainContent$uxProduct$uxProductTabs$ProductTabs$pnlCustomerReviews$uxProductReviews$TopNextLink','')">Next </a> </div> </div> <div class="Spacer"> &nbsp;</div> <div> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_lblErrorMsg"></span></div> <div class="Spacer"> &nbsp;</div> </div> </div> </div> </div><div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlAdditionalInformation" class="ajax__tab_panel" style="display:none;visibility:hidden;"> <div class="ShippingInfo"> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlAdditionalInformation_ProductAdditionalInformation">This firearm ships to your local gun dealer/gun store (FFL dealer).
